Remove chicken and set aside 🍗.&quot;],[0,&quot;Add the chopped onion to the pot and cook 4–5 minutes until translucent, then stir in the minced garlic and cook 30 seconds 🧅🧄.&quot;],[0,&quot;Stir in the chopped sun-dried tomatoes and Italian seasoning, cooking 1–2 minutes to release their flavor 🍅🌿.&quot;],[0,&quot;If using, pour in the white wine to deglaze the pan, scraping up browned bits; simmer 1–2 minutes to reduce 🍷.&quot;],[0,&quot;Add the chicken broth and return the seared chicken breasts to the pot. Bring to a gentle simmer, cover, and cook 12–15 minutes until chicken reaches 75°C / done 🍲.&quot;],[0,&quot;Remove the chicken and shred or chop into bite-sized pieces with two forks. Return the chicken to the pot.&quot;],[0,&quot;Reduce heat to low. Stir in the heavy cream and grated Parmesan until melted and creamy. If you want a thicker soup, whisk in the cornstarch slurry and simmer 2–3 minutes until slightly thickened 🥛🧀.&quot;],[0,&quot;Add the fresh spinach, red pepper flakes (if using), and lemon juice. Stir until greens wilt and everything is heated through 🌱🍋.&quot;],[0,&quot;Taste and adjust seasoning with salt and pepper.
